**REQUIRED WORKFLOW:**
1. FIRST use Sourcegraph tools (keyword_search, finder, list_files) to explore the codebase structure and find relevant code
2. Use go_to_definition and find_references to trace code relationships
3. After finding code via Sourcegraph, use Read to verify actual local contents before editing
4. If Sourcegraph shows different code than local, TRUST THE LOCAL CODE
5. Use `deepsearch` for complex architectural questions — it returns a polling link, NOT immediate results
6. After calling `deepsearch`, continue working with other tools for 30-60 seconds, then call `deepsearch_read` with the polling link
7. Retry `deepsearch_read` at least 3 times (Deep Search takes 50-120 seconds to complete)

# Investigation: DRA AllocationMode API Change Impact Analysis

**Repository:** kubernetes/kubernetes
**Task Type:** Impact Analysis (investigation only — no code changes)

## Scenario

The Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) scheduler plugin is being modified to allow `AllocationMode: All` from multi-node resource pools. Previously, this allocation mode was restricted to single-node pools only. Before this change ships, the team needs a comprehensive impact analysis.

## Your Task

Produce an impact analysis report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:
1. All source files that reference `AllocationMode` or the DRA allocation logic
2. Which controllers and schedulers are affected
3. What test files cover the current allocation behavior
4. What performance implications exist (scheduler hot paths affected)
5. Which downstream consumers (kubelet, device plugins) would see changed behavior
6. Risk assessment: what could break if this change has bugs

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Scope of the change — what components are affected and why>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted, categorized by risk level>

## Recommendation
<Risk mitigation strategy and testing plan>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT write any code
- Do NOT modify any source files
- Your job is investigation and analysis only
- Focus on tracing `AllocationMode` through the DRA plugin, scheduler framework, and kubelet

    52→// GatherPools collects information about all resource pools which provide
    53→// devices that are accessible from the given node.
    54→//
    55→// Out-dated slices are silently ignored. Pools may be incomplete (not all
    56→// required slices available) or invalid (for example, device names not unique).
    57→// Both is recorded in the result.
    58→func GatherPools(ctx context.Context, slices []*resourceapi.ResourceSlice, node *v1.Node, features Features) ([]*Pool, error) {
    59→	slicesByPool := make(map[poolIdentifier][]*resourceapi.ResourceSlice)
    60→	for _, slice := range slices {
    61→		poolID := poolIdentifier{
    62→			driver: slice.Spec.Driver,
    63→			pool:   slice.Spec.Pool.Name,
    64→		}
    65→		slicesByPool[poolID] = append(slicesByPool[poolID], slice)
    66→	}
    67→
    68→	// We need to check whether a pool is complete while we have all
    69→	// the slices. Once we discard slices that don't target the node, we
    70→	// no longer have the information needed to find out.
    71→	incompletePools := sets.New[poolIdentifier]()
    72→	for poolID, slices := range slicesByPool {
    73→		complete := true
    74→		sliceCount := len(slices)
    75→		generation := slices[0].Spec.Pool.Generation
    76→		for _, slice := range slices {
    77→			// If the number of slices in the pool specified in any of the slices
    78→			// doesn't match what we found, the pool is most likely being updated
    79→			// by the controller.
    80→			if slice.Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount != int64(sliceCount) {
    81→				complete = false
    82→			}
    83→			// If the generation of the pool isn't the same across all slices,
    84→			// the pool is most likely being updated by the controller. We can't
    85→			// allocate device
... (truncated)

   184→func poolIsInvalid(pool *Pool) (bool, string) {
   185→	devices := sets.New[draapi.UniqueString]()
   186→	for _, slice := range pool.Slices {
   187→		for _, device := range slice.Spec.Devices {
   188→			if devices.Has(device.Name) {
   189→				return true, fmt.Sprintf("duplicate device name %s", device.Name)
   190→			}
   191→			devices.Insert(device.Name)
   192→		}
   193→	}
   194→	return false, ""
   195→}

146-assistanttext-
The investigation report has been written to `/logs/agent/investigation.md`. Here's a summary of the key findings:

**Core Change:** Commit `2e534d6` modifies `GatherPools` in all 3 allocator variants (stable/incubating/experimental) to pre-compute pool completeness across *all* slices before node filtering, enabling `AllocationMode: All` with multi-node pools. Previously, pools spanning multiple nodes appeared "incomplete" after node filtering, blocking All-mode allocation.

**Known Issue:** This change was **reverted in `a0e500a`** due to a confirmed performance regression. The extra O(N) pass over all ResourceSlices in `GatherPools` runs for every candidate node during scheduler filtering, creating significant overhead at scale (e.g., 500 nodes × 2000 slices = 1M extra iterations per scheduling cycle).

**Blast Radius:**
- **High risk:** `GatherPools` in `pools_{stable,incubating,experimental}.go` and the scheduler `dynamicresources.go` Filter path
- **Medium risk:** The `allocateOne()` function's All-mode code path, validation, and quota evaluator
- **Low risk:** Kubelet, device plugins, and resource claim controller — they don't interpret `AllocationMode`

**Recommendation:** Do not ship this implementation. The later HEAD code in the repository uses a smarter lazy approach (`checkSlicesInPool`) that only scans all slices when a pool appears incomplete after node filtering, avoiding the upfront O(N) cost. The report includes a detailed testing plan for any re-implementation.

The map is indexed by device\n\t// and its values represent for which of a pod's claims the device will\n\t// be allocated.\n\t// Claims are identified by their index in claimsToAllocate.\n\tallocatingDevices map[DeviceID]sets.Set[int]\n\tresult            []internalAllocationResult\n}\n\n// counterSets is a map with the name of counter sets to the counters in\n// the set.\ntype counterSets map[draapi.UniqueString]map[string]resourceapi.Counter\n\n// matchKey identifies a device/request pair.\ntype matchKey struct {\n\tDeviceID\n\trequestIndices\n}\n\n// requestIndices identifies one specific request\n// or subrequest by three properties:\n//",

  "content": "# Investigation Report\n\n## Summary\n\nThe change in commit `2e534d6` modifies the `GatherPools` function in all three allocator variants (stable, incubating, experimental) to pre-compute pool completeness across *all* slices before filtering by node, enabling `AllocationMode: All` to work with multi-node resource pools. This change was later reverted in `a0e500a` due to a performance regression caused by iterating all slices twice in `GatherPools`. The scope is narrow (4 files, ~160 added lines), but the blast radius spans the entire DRA scheduling hot path and affects every pod that uses structured resource claims.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nPreviously, `GatherPools` determined pool completeness *after* filtering slices by node affinity. For a multi-node resource pool (e.g., pool with 2 slices targeting different nodes), only the slices matching the current node were retained. The pool appeared \"incomplete\" (1 of 2 expected slices), causing `AllocationMode: All` to fail with \"resource pool is currently being updated\" even when the pool was healthy.\n\nThe fix pre-computes completeness by:\n1. Grouping all slices by `(driver, pool)` into a `slicesByPool` map before any node filtering\n2. Checking `ResourceSliceCount` and `Generation` consistency across all slices in the pool\n3. Storing incomplete pool identifiers in an `incompletePools` set\n4. Using that set (instead of post-filter slice count) when marking `Pool.IsIncomplete`\n\nThis approach introduces a **new O(N) pass over all slices** at the top of `GatherPools`, where N is the total number of ResourceSlices in the cluster (not just those matching the current node).\n\n### Components affected:\n- **`GatherPools`** in `pools_stable.go`, `pools_incubating.go`, `pools_experimental.go` \u2014 the core change\n- **`allocator_stable.go` / `allocator_incubating.go` / `allocator_experimental.go`** \u2014 consume pools; the `AllocationMode: All` code path in `allocateOne()` now operates on pools that may span multiple nodes\n- **Scheduler plugin** (`dynamicresources.go`) \u2014 calls `structured.NewAllocator` \u2192 `Allocator.Allocate` \u2192 `GatherPools` on every `Filter` invocation per candidate node\n- **Resource quota evaluator** (`resource_claims.go`) \u2014 uses `AllocationResultsMaxSize` for worst-case \"All\" mode quota; unaffected by the pool change\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Changed files (commit `2e534d6da10`)\n\n| File | Lines Changed | Role |\n|------|-------------|------|\n| `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/pools_stable.go:45-148` | +43/-2 | Core `GatherPools` change: pre-compute `incompletePools` set |\n| `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating/pools_incubating.go:45-140` | +43/-2 | Same change for incubating allocator |\n| `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental/pools_experimental.go:45-162` | +43/-2 | Same change for experimental allocator |\n| `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:5090-5129` | +34/-0 | New test: `allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool` |\n\n### Key code paths\n\n1. **Pool completeness check (the change)** \u2014 `pools_stable.go:59-95`:\n   - Creates `slicesByPool` map grouping *all* slices before node filtering\n   - Iterates each pool checking `ResourceSliceCount` vs actual count and `Generation` consistency\n   - Records incomplete pools in `sets.New[poolIdentifier]()`\n\n2. **Incomplete pool check after filtering** \u2014 `pools_stable.go:142-143`:\n   ```go\n   pool.IsIncomplete = incompletePools.Has(poolIdentifier{driver: pool.Driver.String(), pool: pool.Pool.String()})\n   ```\n   Changed from the prior: `pool.IsIncomplete = int64(len(pool.Slices)) != pool.Slices[0].Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount`\n\n3. **AllocationMode All rejection of incomplete pools** \u2014 `allocator_stable.go:455-461`:\n   ```go\n   for _, pool := range pools {\n       if pool.IsIncomplete {\n           return requestData, fmt.Errorf(\"claim %s, request %s: asks for all devices, but resource pool %s is currently being updated\", ...)\n       }\n   ```\n   This existing code now allows multi-node pools through because `IsIncomplete` is only true when the *global* slice count doesn't match.\n\n4. **Scheduler Filter hot path** \u2014 `dynamicresources.go:561-570`:\n   ```go\n   slices, err := pl.draManager.ResourceSlices().ListWithDeviceTaintRules()\n   features := AllocatorFeatures(pl.fts)\n   allocator, err := structured.NewAllocator(ctx, features, *allocatedState, pl.draManager.DeviceClasses(), slices, pl.celCache)\n   ```\n   This creates a new allocator per scheduling cycle. `GatherPools` is then called inside `Allocate()` (line 129 of `allocator_stable.go`) for every candidate node.\n\n5. **Kubelet DRA manager** \u2014 `pkg/kubelet/cm/dra/manager.go:397-402`:\n   The kubelet receives the `AllocationResult` via the ResourceClaim status and calls `NodePrepareResources` on the DRA driver plugin. It does **not** interpret `AllocationMode` \u2014 it only processes the allocated device results. Therefore, the kubelet is not directly affected by this change, but it will receive allocation results that span devices from only the node-local subset of a multi-node pool.\n\n### Test coverage\n\n| change: 2-slice pool across 2 nodes, allocates only node1's device |\n| `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:3680` | `prioritized-list-allocation-mode-all` | AllocationMode All with prioritized list subrequests |\n| `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:3844` | `prioritized-list-max-allocation-allocation-mode-all` | Max allocation size with All mode |\n| `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:2484` | `prioritized-list-subrequests-with-allocation-mode-all` | Subrequests with All mode |\n| `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:4629-4750` | perf benchmark for All mode from multi-node pools (performance regression risk)\n- No test for the race condition where slices are being updated while `GatherPools` is iterating\n\n## Affected Components\n\n### HIGH RISK\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `pools_stable.go:58-148` | Core `GatherPools` change. Performance regression confirmed (caused revert `a0e500a`). Extra O(N) slice iteration on every `Allocate()` call per node. |\n| `structured/internal/incubating` | `pools_incubating.go:58-140` | Same change for incubating variant |\n| `structured/internal/experimental` | `pools_experimental.go:58-162` | Same change for experimental variant |\n| `scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources` | `dynamicresources.go:561-570` | Calls `NewAllocator`\u2192`Allocate`\u2192`GatherPools` per candidate node during Filter. Performance regression multiplied by number of nodes. |\n\n### MEDIUM RISK\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:446-480` | `allocateOne()` with `doAllDevices=true`: now iterates over node-local devices from multi-node pools. If pool is incorrectly marked complete when it isn't, \"All\" mode will allocate a subset, violating the semantic. |\n| `structured/internal/incubating` | `allocator_incubating.go:982-985` | Same as above for incubating |\n| `structured/internal/experimental` | `allocator_experimental.go:982-985` | Same as above for experimental |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/validation` | `validation.go:268-286` | Validation allows `AllocationMode: All` but does not validate pool topology; no change needed but adds context |\n| `pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core` | `resource_claims.go:249-277` | Quota uses `AllocationResultsMaxSize` for All mode worst case. Multi-node pools don't change this, but if pool sizes grow, quota might under-count. |\n\n### LOW RISK\n\n| Package | File | Impact |\n|---------|------|--------|\n| `pkg/controller/resourceclaim` | `controller.go:936-940` | Resource claim controller: deallocates by clearing `Status.Allocation`. Agnostic to allocation mode. |\n| `pkg/kubelet/cm/dra` | `manager.go:397-402` | Kubelet DRA manager: receives `AllocationResult`, calls `NodePrepareResources`. Does not interpret `AllocationMode`. No behavioral change. |\n| `kubeletplugin/draplugin.go:856-858` | Kubelet plugin | `NodePrepareResources` implementation. Processes device list from allocation result. No AllocationMode awareness. |\n| `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1143-1150` | API types | `DeviceAllocationMode` enum. No change. |\n| `client-go/applyconfigurations/resource/v1/` | Apply configs | Generated code. No behavioral change. |\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Known Risk: Performance Regression\nThis exact change was **already reverted** in commit `a0e500a` with message: *\"It caused a performance regression, a different fix is needed.\"* The performance issue is the additional `O(N)` pass in `GatherPools` over all slices (line 59-95), where `N` is the total number of `ResourceSlice` objects cluster-wide. This runs for **every candidate node** during scheduler filtering. For clusters with 500 nodes and 2000 resource slices, this adds ~500 * 2000 = 1M extra iterations per scheduling cycle.\n\n### Risk Mitigation Strategy\n\n1. **Do not ship this implementation as-is.** The revert confirms the approach has a measurable performance penalty. A different strategy is needed.\n\n2. **Alternative approaches to investigate:**\n   - **Pre-index pools by `(driver, pool)` at informer level** instead of re-computing on every `GatherPools` call. The `ResourceSliceTracker` used by the scheduler could maintain a pool completeness cache.\n   - **Lazy completeness check**: only invoke the expensive `checkSlicesInPool` scan (as seen in the Sourcegraph HEAD implementation at `pools_stable.go:128-157`) when a pool appears incomplete after node filtering, rather than pre-computing for all pools. This is the approach taken in the later HEAD code.\n   - **Limit the extra pass to claims that actually use `AllocationMode: All`**: skip the `slicesByPool` grouping when no claim requires it.\n\n3. **Testing plan for any re-implementation:**\n   - Add a scheduler perf benchmark in `test/integration/scheduler_perf/dra/` with:\n     - Multi-node resource pools (10+ nodes, 200+ slices per pool)\n     - Claims using `AllocationMode: All` and `AllocationMode: ExactCount`\n     - Measure p99 filter latency before and after the change\n   - Add E2E test in `test/e2e/dra/dra.go` for multi-node pool with `AllocationMode: All`\n   - Add unit test for the race condition: pool slices being updated during `GatherPools`\n   - Add unit test for mixed pools: some node-local, some multi-node, with `AllocationMode: All`\n\n4. **Correctness verification:** The `allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool` test (line 5503 in allocator_testing.go) is the right shape, but needs companion tests for:\n   - Incomplete multi-node pool (one slice missing) \u2192 allocation should fail\n   - Multi-node pool with generation mismatch \u2192 allocation should fail\n   - Multiple All-mode requests across different multi-node pools\n   - All-mode request where node has 0 matching devices in the multi-node pool\n\n5. **Downstream impact is minimal.** The kubelet, device plugins, and resource claim controller do not interpret `AllocationMode` and are agnostic to whether devices came from a node-local or multi-node pool. The scheduler plugin and quota evaluator are the primary consumers.\n",

The `ResourceSliceTracker` used by the scheduler could maintain a pool completeness cache.\n   - **Lazy completeness check**: only invoke the expensive `checkSlicesInPool` scan (as seen in the Sourcegraph HEAD implementation at `pools_stable.go:128-157`) when a pool appears incomplete after node filtering, rather than pre-computing for all pools. The scheduler plugin and quota evaluator are the primary consumers.\n",

1. WRITE /logs/agent/investigation.md
# Investigation Report

## Summary

The change in commit `2e534d6` modifies the `GatherPools` function in all three allocator variants (stable, incubating, experimental) to pre-compute pool completeness across *all* slices before filtering by node, enabling `AllocationMode: All` to work with multi-node resource pools. This change was later reverted in `a0e500a` due to a performance regression caused by iterating all slices twice in `GatherPools`. The scope is narrow (4 files, ~160 added lines), but the blast radius spans the entire DRA scheduling hot path and affects every pod that uses structured resource claims.

## Root Cause

Previously, `GatherPools` determined pool completeness *after* filtering slices by node affinity. For a multi-node resource pool (e.g., pool with 2 slices targeting different nodes), only the slices matching the current node were retained. The pool appeared "incomplete" (1 of 2 expected slices), causing `AllocationMode: All` to fail with "resource pool is currently being updated" even when the pool was healthy.

The fix pre-computes completeness by:
1. Grouping all slices by `(driver, pool)` into a `slicesByPool` map before any node filtering
2. Checking `ResourceSliceCount` and `Generation` consistency across all slices in the pool
3. Storing incomplete pool identifiers in an `incompletePools` set
4. Using that set (instead of post-filter slice count) when marking `Pool.IsIncomplete`

This approach introduces a **new O(N) pass over all slices** at the top of `GatherPools`, where N is the total number of ResourceSlices in the cluster (not just those matching the current node).

### Components affected:
- **`GatherPools`** in `pools_stable.go`, `pools_incubating.go`, `pools_experimental.go` — the core change
- **`allocator_stable.go` / `allocato
... (truncated)
